The hotel consists of the Lijiang Guanfang Hotel Flagship Store and the property-right hotels - Guanfang "Garden Villa" and "Hotel Villa" property-right hotels, with a total of 1,228 guest rooms; the flagship store opened on January 18, 1998 and was partially renovated in 2004. The Garden Villa and Hotel Villa opened in October 2003.
Lijiang Guanfang Hotel Flagship Store is a five-star hotel with modern comprehensive service facilities. It is located in the prime location at the southern end of Shangri-La Avenue, connected to the Municipal Square in the north, and the world cultural heritage - Lijiang Ancient Town is an eight-minute walk to the southeast. It is closely connected to Lijiang's prosperous commercial street in the south; Lijiang Guanfang Hotel Flagship Store has 288 high-end rooms. It was officially opened on January 18, 1998 and is the first five-star hotel in Yunnan. It was once the designated reception unit for international competitions such as the "International Seven Star Cross-Country Race", and has successfully received a large number of former leaders of various depar**ents of the country, such as former President Jiang Zemin, Premier Zhu Rongji, etc., former Chief Executive of the Hong Kong Special Administrative Region Tung Chee-hwa, and foreign guests. The hotel has Chinese and Western restaurants, bars, indoor swimming pools, saunas, bowling alleys, dance halls, business centers, conference rooms, and an international conference hall that can accommodate 400 people at the same time.

posted:Posted March 8, 2024
msg:Before choosing this hotel, I was attracted by the five-star service reviews from other guests. Unfortunately, my actual experience was very different from these reviews. From the moment I stepped into the hotel, I felt the lack of service. When checking in, the front desk staff seemed more focused on chatting with people than greeting incoming guests, which made me feel rather awkward while I waited.

In addition, there is a lack of necessary guidance in the hotel. For example, there are no obvious signs in the breakfast area, making people feel helpless when searching. For a traveler looking forward to receiving travel advice and local guides, the hotel also fell short in providing assistance.

As for the facilities, although it can be seen that they have definitely stood the test of time, unfortunately, they do not seem to have been maintained and updated as much as they should. These old facilities are far from the five star standards I expected.

Nevertheless, I must admit that considering the price of 300 yuan per night, the conditions of this hotel seem to be worthy of its price. But for those travelers who expect five-star service, they may need to readjust their expectations or choose other accommodation options. Overall, this was a lesson that reminded me to pay more attention to the actual experience rather than just the ratings when booking a hotel.
